Cargo 1.94 (2026-03-05)

2c283a9a‚Ä¶rust-1.94.0

Ï∂îÍ∞ÄÎê®

  • üéâ Stabilize the config include key. The top-level include config key allows loading additional config files, enabling better organization, sharing, and management of Cargo configurations across projects and environments. docs #16284
  • üéâ Stabilize the pubtime field in registry index. This records when a crate version was published and enables time-based dependency resolution in the future. Note that crates.io will gradually backfill existing packages when a new version is published. Not all crates have pubtime yet. #16369 #16372
  • Cargo now parses TOML v1.1 for manifests and configuration files. Note that using these features in Cargo.toml will raise your development MSRV, but the published manifest remains compatible with older parsers. #16415
  • The timing HTML report now has a new SVG rendering option for a better rendering performance with large builds. Canvas rendering is still available but will be phased out. #15091
  • The CARGO_BIN_EXE_<name> environment variable is now available at runtime not just compile time. #16421
  • perf: Optimize cargo clean with multiple --package specifiers. #16264
  • perf: Optimize cargo locate-project --workspace by avoiding full workspace loading when only the workspace root path is needed. #16423

Î≥ÄÍ≤ΩÎê®

  • Improve error message when Cargo build target source files are missing. #16338
  • Improve error message for missing dependencies using rustc diagnostic style. #16500
  • Display where the patch was defined in patch-related error messages. #16407
  • List all available features when the requested feature has no close match. #16445
  • Display lockfile path in very verbose mode -vv) when waiting on a file lock. #16491
  • cargo-new: Improve quality of package name error messages. #16398

ÏàòÏ†ïÎê®

  • Don‚Äôt read config file twice when $CARGO_HOME is a symlinked directory. #16325
  • cargo-info: default to inspecting local package when no registry is explicitly specified. #16358
  • cargo-info: resolve underscore vs hyphen mismatch in schema lookup. #16455
  • cargo-package: skip registry verification when using --list. #16341
  • cargo-package: detect dirty files when run from workspace member directory. #16479
  • cargo-vendor: recursively filter .gitattributes and .gitignores in subdirectories. Previously only top-level Git files were filtered, causing checksum failures when vendored code is committed to a Git repository. #16439
  • cargo-vendor: unpack from local-registry cache path correctly. #16435

ÎÇòÏù¥ÌãÄÎ¶¨(Nightly) Ï†ÑÏö©

  • üî• -Zany-build-script-metadata: Allow any build script to emit cargo::metadata=KEY=VALUE and expose it to dependents via CARGO_DEP_<name>_<key> environment variables. docs #16436 #16486 #16489 #16494 #16496
  • timings: Remove --timings=<FMT> optional format values. The -Zbuild-analysis logging is now the recommended approach for machine-readable timing data. Use the unstable cargo report timings to generate HTML reports. #16420
  • -Zlockfile-path: Add new resolver.lockfile-path config to replace CLI --lockfile-path option. --lockfile-path CLI option will be removed in a future release. #16510
  • -Zbuild-analysis: new cargo report rebuilds command to analyze rebuild reasons from previous sessions. #16408 #16456
  • -Zbuild-analysis: new cargo report sessions command to list build session IDs. #16428
  • -Zbuild-analysis: new cargo report timings command for HTML replay. #16346 #16350 #16352 #16377 #16378 #16382 #16390 #16414 #16441 #16448 #16485 #16490
  • -Zbuild-dir: implement fine-grained unit-level locking for build cache. #16155
  • -Zbuild-dir-new-layout: move build script binaries to deps directory. #16515
  • -Zbuild-dir-new-layout: do not create examples dir when using new layout. #16514
  • -Zbuild-dir-new-layout: remove hashes from bins in new layout. #16351
  • -Zbuild-dir-new-layout: use unit_id, not pkg hash, for bin/lib pkg_dirs. #16345
  • -Zbuild-dir-new-layout: include all search paths with new build layout. #16348
  • -Zcargo-lints: add Clippy-like lint groups. #16464
  • -Zcargo-lints: new implicit_minimum_version_req lint. #16321
  • -Zno-embed-metadata: invalidate the whole build cache when the flag changes. #16513
  • -Zsbom: don‚Äôt set CARGO_SBOM_PATH when empty. #16419

Î¨∏ÏÑú

  • Clarify that OUT_DIR is not cleaned between builds. #16437
  • Document the only possible values for DEBUG in build scripts. #16413
  • Add best practice for how to check in generated files. #16405
  • Document more services and permissions of the Cargo team. #16402
  • FAQ: Include an entry on disk space. #16349

ÎÇ¥Î∂Ä Î≥ÄÍ≤Ω

  • Cache Git submodules into the Git database for faster subsequent fetches. #16246
  • Fixed Git partial OIDs being incorrectly zero-padded. #16511
  • Migrate some cases to expect/reason. #16461
  • Support in-memory only Manifest for libcargo #16409
  • cargo-test-support: Use test name for dir when running tests. #16121
  • test: Use a larger default term width. #16403 #16391
  • test: Adjust output for out-of-tree build-dir. #16343
  • test: update to proc_macro::tracked::path. #16380

Cargo 1.93 (2026-01-22)

344c4567‚Ä¶rust-1.93.0

Ï∂îÍ∞ÄÎê®

  • Enable CARGO_CFG_DEBUG_ASSERTIONS environment variable in build scripts based on profile settings. #16160
  • Add support for completing --config values in Bash #16245
  • cargo-clean: Add --workspace flag to clean artifacts of the workspace members. #16263
  • cargo-tree: Support long forms for --format variables #16204

Î≥ÄÍ≤ΩÎê®

  • ‚ùóÔ∏è cargo publish no longer keeps .crate tarballs as final build artifacts even when the build.build-dir config is unset. #15915
  • Migrate more diagnostic formatting to rustc-like style (annotate-snippets style) #16143
  • Point out when a key belongs to Cargo configuration when seeing an unused field in Cargo manifest. #16256
  • When failing to update or create lockfile, provide clearer context and suggested user actions to help resolve it. #16233 #16227
  • Emit helpful error messages when GitHub pull request URLs are used as dependencies in the manifest. #16207
  • Avoid unnecessary artifact directory locking for check builds. #16230 #16299 #16307 #16385 #16386
  • Refer to commands, not subcommands in CLI help text. #16226
  • cargo-install: Cargo treated a relative path in install.root without a trailing slash as relative path to the current working directory. This case will now get a deprecation warning. It was an oversight and will be changed to config-relative path like other config fields in the future. #16125
  • cargo-package: Suppress missing metadata warnings for non-crates.io publishable packages #16241
  • cargo-publish: emit a warning when both package.publish and --index are specified #16268
  • cargo-run: in help text, teach how to escape arguments to be forwarded literally to an underlying program #16225

ÏàòÏ†ïÎê®

  • Zsh shell completion variables no longer leak into user‚Äôs environment #16144
  • Fixed Cargo generating dep-info file with invalid trailing backslashes on Windows. #16223
  • Fixed non-mergeable list from --config CLI being overridden by environment variables. #16220
  • Fixed nested non-mergeable list from --config CLI got merged with other configurations. #16219
  • Cargo now updates mtime for files generated by cargo package after unpacking .crate source tarballs. This ensures files do not have overly old mtime that some zip tools can‚Äôt handle. #16250
  • Shift mtime for cargo check artifacts (.rmeta files). This addresses a regression in rustc incremental compilation skipping unnecessary rmeta generation but didn‚Äôt update mtime for existing rmeta files. #16262
  • cargo-doc: clean generated doc directories for only requested targets. Previously when rustc version mismatches, Cargo removes all generated doc directories including target platforms that are not part of the build. #16331
  • cargo-install: fix out-of-bound error in crate name validation #16314
  • cargo-package: generated files in tarball should have deterministic timestamp. #16242
  • cargo-package: exclude target/package directory from backups via CACHEDIR.TAG. #16272
  • cargo-vendor: fix panic on Windows caused by fallback of fs::rename. #16214

ÎÇòÏù¥ÌãÄÎ¶¨(Nightly) Ï†ÑÏö©

  • üî• -Zrustdoc-mergeable-info leverages rustdoc‚Äôs mergeable crate info, so cargo doc can merge cross-crate information (like the search index, source files index) from separate output directories, and run rustdoc in parallel. docs #16309
  • üî• cargo generate-lockfile now has an unstable --publish-time flag that package resolution will not consider any package newer than the specified time. This is not useful until registry index starts including the pubtime field. #16265
  • build-plan: Remove the unstable feature build-plan entirely. The Cargo team are looking forward to other alternatives like plumbing commands, `--unit-graph, and structured logging helping to fill the gap. #16212

Cargo 1.91 (2025-10-30)

840b83a1‚Ä¶rust-1.91.0

Ï∂îÍ∞ÄÎê®

  • üéâ Stabilize build.build-dir. This config sets the directory where intermediate build artifacts are stored. These artifacts are produced by Cargo and rustc during the build process. End users usually won‚Äôt need to interact with them, and the layout inside build-dir is an implementation detail that may change without notice. (config doc) (build cache doc) #15833 #15840
  • The --target flag and the build.target configuration can now take literal "host-tuple" string, which will internally be substituted by the host machine‚Äôs target triple. #15838 #16003 #16032

Î≥ÄÍ≤ΩÎê®

  • ‚ùóÔ∏è cargo publish no longer keeps .crate tarballs as final build artifacts when build.build-dir is set. These tarballs were previously included due to an oversight and are now treated as intermediate artifacts. To get .crate tarballs as final artifacts, use cargo package. In a future version, this change will apply regardless of build.build-dir. #15910
  • Adjust Cargo messages to match rustc diagnostic style #15928
  • More helpful error for invalid cargo-features = [] #15781
  • Don‚Äôt stop at first error when emitting lints and warnings #15889
  • Show the bad manifest path in the error message #15896
  • Suggest workspace hints for invalid boolean dependencies #15507
  • cargo-package: Always reuse the workspace‚Äôs target-dir during the package verification. Previously Cargo created a new standalone target directory within the unpacked source. #15783
  • cargo-publish: Add more context to publish-failed error message #15879

ÏàòÏ†ïÎê®

ÎÇòÏù¥ÌãÄÎ¶¨(Nightly) Ï†ÑÏö©

  • üî• -Zsection-timings extend the output of cargo build --timings. It tells rustc to produce timings of individual compilation sections, which will be then displayed in the timings HTML/JSON output. (docs) #15780 #15923
  • üî• -Zbuild-dir-new-layout enables the new build-dir filesystem layout, which unblocks work towards caching and locking improvements. (docs) (project goal) #15848
  • üî• -Zbuild-analysis records and persists detailed build metrics (timings, rebuild reasons, etc.) across runs, with new commands to query past builds. (docs) (project goal) #15845
  • multiple-build-scripts: Accessing each build script‚Äôs OUT_DIR and in the correct order #15776
  • -Zcargo-lints: Linting system infra improvement #15865
  • -Zscript: Cover some frontmatter corner cases #15886
  • -Zscript: Match test updates in rustc #15878
  • -Zscript: Switch frontmatter tests to end-to-end #15899

  • -Zscript: Pull out as a dedicated mod #15914

Cargo 1.90 (2025-09-18)

c24e1064‚Ä¶rust-1.90.0

Ï∂îÍ∞ÄÎê®

  • üéâ Stabilize multi-package publishing. This allows cargo to publish multiple crates in a workspace, even if they have inter-dependencies. For example, cargo publish --workspace or cargo publish -p foo -p bar. Note that cargo publish is still non-atomic at this time. If there is a server side error during the publish, the workspace will be left in a partially published state. #15636 #15711

Cargo 1.89 (2025-08-07)

873a0649‚Ä¶rust-1.89.0

Ï∂îÍ∞ÄÎê®

  • Add * and ? pattern support for SSH known hosts matching. #15508
  • Stabilize doctest-xcompile. Doctests will now automatically be tested when cross-compiling to a target that is different from the host, just like other tests. #15462

Î≥ÄÍ≤ΩÎê®

  • ‚ùóÔ∏è cargo fix and cargo clippy --fix now run only on the default Cargo targets by default, matching the behavior of cargo check. To run on all Cargo targets, use the --all-targets flag. This change aligns the behavior with other commands. Edition flags like --edition and --edition-idioms remain implying --all-targets by default. #15192
  • Respect Retry-After header for HTTP 429 responses when talking to registries. #15463
  • Improved error message for the CRATE[@<VER>] argument prefixed with v. #15484
  • Improved error message for the CRATE[@<VER>] argument with invalid package name characters. #15441
  • cargo-add: suggest similarly named features #15438

ÏàòÏ†ïÎê®

  • Fixed potential deadlock in CacheState::lock #15698 #15699
  • Fixed the --manifest-path arg being ignored in cargo fix #15633
  • When publishing, don‚Äôt tell people to ctrl-c without knowing consequences. #15632
  • Added missing --offline in shell completions. #15623
  • cargo-credential-libsecret: load libsecret only once #15295
  • When failing to find the mtime of a file for rebuild detection, report an explicit reason rather than ‚Äústale; unknown reason‚Äù. #15617
  • Fixed cargo add overwriting symlinked Cargo.toml files #15281
  • Vendor files with .rej/.orig suffix #15569
  • Vendor using direct extraction for registry sources. This should ensure that vendored files now always match the originals. #15514
  • In the network retry message, use singular ‚Äútry‚Äù for the last retry. #15328

ÎÇòÏù¥ÌãÄÎ¶¨(Nightly) Ï†ÑÏö©

  • üî• -Zno-embed-metadata: This tells Cargo to pass the -Zembed-metadata=no flag to the compiler, which instructs it not to embed metadata within rlib and dylib artifacts. In this case, the metadata will only be stored in .rmeta files. (docs) #15378
  • üî• Plumb rustc -Zhint-mostly-unused flag through as a profile option (docs) #15643
  • Added the ‚Äúfuture‚Äù edition #15595
  • Added -Zfix-edition #15596

  • -Zscript: Make cargo script ignore workspaces. #15496

Cargo 1.88 (2025-06-26)

a6c604d1‚Ä¶rust-1.88.0

Ï∂îÍ∞ÄÎê®

  • üéâ Stabilize automatic garbage collection for global caches.

    When building, Cargo downloads and caches crates needed as dependencies. Historically, these downloaded files would never be cleaned up, leading to an unbounded amount of disk usage in Cargo‚Äôs home directory. In this version, Cargo introduces a garbage collection mechanism to automatically clean up old files (e.g. .crate files). Cargo will remove files downloaded from the network if not accessed in 3 months, and files obtained from the local system if not accessed in 1 month. Note that this automatic garbage collection will not take place if running offline (using --offline or --frozen).

    Cargo 1.78 and newer track the access information needed for this garbage collection. If you regularly use versions of Cargo older than 1.78, in addition to running current versions of Cargo, and you expect to have some crates accessed exclusively by the older versions of Cargo and don‚Äôt want to re-download those crates every ~3 months, you may wish to set cache.auto-clean-frequency = "never" in the Cargo configuration. (docs) #14287

  • Allow boolean literals as cfg predicates in Cargo.toml and configurations. For example, [target.'cfg(not(false))'.dependencies] is a valid cfg predicate. (RFC 3695) #14649

  • Don‚Äôt canonicalize executable path for the CARGO environment variable. #15355

  • Suggest similar looking feature names when feature is missing. #15454
  • Use zlib-rs for gzip (de)compression for .crate tarballs. #15417
